Page 362 

015901,002860: 
015902,002861:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015903,002862: 
015904,002863:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015905,002864: 
015906,002865:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015907,002866:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015908,002867:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015909,002868:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015910,002869: 
015911,002870:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015912,002871:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015913,002872:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015914,002873: 
015915,002874:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015916,002875:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015917,002876:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015918,002877:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015919,002878:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015920,002879:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015921,002880:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015922,002881:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015923,002882:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015924,002883:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015925,002884:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015926,002885: 
015927,002886: 40,3362           44710        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015928,002887: 40,3363           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015929,002888: 40,3364           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015930,002889: 40,3365           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015931,002890: 40,3366           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015932,002891: 40,3367           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015933,002892: 40,3370           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015934,002893: 40,3371           03400                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015935,002894: 40,3372           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015936,002895: 40,3373           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015937,002896: 40,3374           03376                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015938,002897: 40,3375           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015939,002898: 40,3376           04574                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015940,002899: 40,3377           21176                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015941,002900: 40,3400           34714        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015942,002901: 40,3401           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015943,002902: 40,3402           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015944,002903: 40,3403           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015945,002904: 40,3404           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015946,002905: 40,3405           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015947,002906: 
015948,002907: 40,3406                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015949,002908:

Page 363 

015951,002910:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015952,002911:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015953,002912:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015954,002913:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015955,002914:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015956,002915: 
015957,002916:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015958,002917:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015959,002918:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015960,002919: 
015961,002920:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015962,002921:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015963,002922: 
015964,002923:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015965,002924:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015966,002925:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015967,002926:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015968,002927:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015969,002928: 
015970,002929:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015971,002930:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015972,002931:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015973,002932:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015974,002933: 
015975,002934:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015976,002935:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015977,002936:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015978,002937:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015979,002938:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015980,002939:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015981,002940:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015982,002941: 
015983,002942:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015984,002943:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015985,002944: 
015986,002945:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015987,002946:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015988,002947: 
015989,002948:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015990,002949:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015991,002950: 
015992,002951:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015993,002952:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015994,002953:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015995,002954:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015996,002955:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015997,002956:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015998,002957:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015999,002958: 
016000,002959:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 364 

016002,002961:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
016003,002962:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
016004,002963:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
016005,002964:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
016006,002965:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
016007,002966:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
016008,002967:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
016009,002968:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
016010,002969:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
016011,002970: 
016012,002971:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
016013,002972:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)

016130,003089:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
016131,003090:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016132,003091: 
016133,003092:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
016134,003093:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016135,003094:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016136,003095:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN  SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016137,003096:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE  SET BY VERB 32
016138,003097: 
016139,003098:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
016140,003099:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016141,003100:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016142,003101:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016143,003102:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016144,003103:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016145,003104:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
016146,003105:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016147,003106:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016148,003107:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.

Page 367 

016150,003109: 
016151,003110:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016152,003111:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016153,003112:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016154,003113:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016155,003114:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016156,003115:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
016157,003116: 
016158,003117:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016159,003118:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016160,003119:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016161,003120:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016162,003121:    4227           74747                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016163,003122:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016164,003123:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
016165,003124:    4232           05070                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016166,003125: 
016167,003126:    4233           05112        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016168,003127: 
016169,003128:    4234           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016170,003129:    4235           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

Page 375 

016497,003456:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016498,003457: 
016499,003458:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016500,003459:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016501,003460:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016502,003461:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016503,003462: 
016504,003463:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016505,003464:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016506,003465:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016507,003466:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016508,003467:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016509,003468:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016510,003469:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016511,003470: 
016512,003471:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016513,003472:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016514,003473:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016515,003474:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016516,003475:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016517,003476: 
016518,003477:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016519,003478:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016520,003479:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016521,003480:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016522,003481:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016523,003482: 
016524,003483:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016525,003484:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016526,003485:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016527,003486:                                                                                                  #        .
016528,003487:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016529,003488:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016530,003489:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016531,003490:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016532,003491: 
016533,003492:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016534,003493:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016535,003494:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016536,003495: 
016537,003496:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016538,003497:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016539,003498:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 376 

016541,003500:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016542,003501: 
016543,003502:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016544,003503:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016545,003504:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016546,003505:    4456           04574        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016547,003506:    4457           10550                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016548,003507:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016549,003508: 
016550,003509:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016551,003510:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016552,003511: 
016553,003512: 04,2550                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016554,003513: 04,2550                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016555,003514: 
016556,003515: 04,2550           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016557,003516: 04,2551           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016558,003517: 04,2552           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016559,003518: 04,2553           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016560,003519: 04,2554           30001                           CA       L                                     
016561,003520: 04,2555           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016562,003521: 04,2556           05070        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016563,003522: 
016564,003523:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016565,003524:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016566,003525:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016567,003526:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016568,003527:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016569,003528: 
016570,003529:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016571,003530:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016572,003531: 
016573,003532:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016574,003533:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016575,003534:    4463           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016576,003535:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016577,003536:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016578,003537:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016579,003538:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016580,003539:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016581,003540:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016582,003541:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016583,003542:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016584,003543: 
016585,003544:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016586,003545:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016587,003546: 
016588,003547:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016589,003548: 
016590,003549:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 377 

016592,003551:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
016593,003552:    4475           44675                           CS       BIT14                                 
016594,003553:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016595,003554:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016596,003555:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016597,003556:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016598,003557:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016599,003558:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016600,003559:    4504           34714                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016601,003560:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016602,003561:    4506           05074                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016603,003562:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
016604,003563:    4510           44706                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
016605,003564:    4511           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
016606,003565:    4512           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
016607,003566:    4513           34714                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016608,003567:    4514           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               
016609,003568:    4515           00144                           TC       RELRET

016731,003690:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016732,003691:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016733,003692:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016734,003693: 
016735,003694:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016736,003695:                                                                                                  #  
016737,003696:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
016738,003697:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016739,003698:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
